  981. # [06:43] <@bz> 9 * This "puppet widget" isn't really a platform widget. It's intended
  982. # [06:43] <@bz> 10 * to be used in widgetless rendering contexts, such as sandboxed
  983. # [06:43] <@bz> 11 * content processes. If any "real" widgetry is needed, the request
  984. # [06:43] <@bz> 12 * is forwarded to and/or data received from elsewhere.
